local function a(b64) 
  local sep=string.char(33).."8".."g" 
  return (b64:gsub(sep..".",""):gsub(".",function(x) 
    if x=='=' then return '' end 
    local f=b:find(x or '') 
    if not f then return '' end 
    local r='' f=f-1 
    for i=6,1,-1 do r=r..(f%2^i-f%2^(i-1)>0 and'1' or'0') end 
    return r end):gsub('%d%d%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?',function(x) 
    if #x~=8 then return '' end 
    local c=0 
    for i=1,8 do c=c+(x:sub(i,i)=='1' and 2^(8-i) or 0) end 
    return string.char(c) end)) 
end 
local function b(s) 
  return (s:gsub('.',function(c) 
    local byte=string.byte(c) 
    if byte>=65 and byte<=90 then return string.char(((byte-65+13)%26)+65) 
    elseif byte>=97 and byte<=122 then return string.char(((byte-97+13)%26)+97) 
    else return c end end)) 
end
